      setDoctorCount(value);
    } else if (e.target.value === '') {
      setDoctorCount(0);

    const value = parseInt(e.target.value, 10);

      nurses: nurseCount,
    };

    // Navigate based on staff count
    if (doctorCount === 1 && nurseCount === 0) {
      // Solo clinic flow
      router.push('/register/hospital/solo');
    } else {
      // Multi-staff flow
      router.push('/register/hospital/admin-check');

const login = async (loginId, password) => {
  const user = await prisma.user.findFirst({ where: { OR: [{ email: loginId }, { phone: loginId }] }, include: { patient: true, doctor: true, hospital: true, nurse: true } });
  if (!user) {
    const nurse = await prisma.nurse.findUnique({ where: { registrationNumber: loginId }, include: { user: true } });
    if (nurse) {
      const userWithRelations = await prisma.user.findUnique({ where: { id: nurse.userId }, include: { patient: true, doctor: true, hospital: true, nurse: true } });
      if (userWithRelations) {
        return handleLoginSuccess(userWithRelations, password);
      }
    }
    throw AppError.unauthorized('Invalid credentials', 'INVALID_CREDENTIALS');
  }
  return handleLoginSuccess(user, password);
};

How to push it to the GitHub without losing the real data?Mar 20Architected GitHub workflow separating code from database dataArchitected GitHub workflow separating code from database dataImportant thing to understand first — the actual data in your PostgreSQL database does NOT go to GitHub and that's correct. What goes to GitHub is:

The code
The migrations (database structure)
The seed files (NMC, CER, INC reference data)

Your teammate runs the migrations and seed on their own machine and gets an identical fresh database. Their data is separate from yours — that's how it should work.

Now here is the exact setup guide to send your teammate. Copy this entire thing and send it to her:

MEDLINK SETUP GUIDE — READ FULLY BEFORE STARTING

You need two repos. Clone both:

git clone https://github.com/vishalp-dev24/medlink-unified-db.git
git clone https://github.com/vishalp-dev24/medlink-id-reg.git

──────────────────────────────────────────
PREREQUISITES
──────────────────────────────────────────
- Node.js 20+
- PostgreSQL 15+
- npm

──────────────────────────────────────────
STEP 1 — Create the database
──────────────────────────────────────────
Open pgAdmin or psql and run:
CREATE DATABASE medlink_db;

──────────────────────────────────────────
STEP 2 — Setup unified database
──────────────────────────────────────────
cd medlink-unified-db

Create a .env file with this content:
DATABASE_URL="postgresql://postgres:YOUR_PASSWORD@localhost:5432/medlink_db"

Replace YOUR_PASSWORD with your PostgreSQL password.

Then run:
npm install
npx prisma migrate deploy
npx ts-node prisma/seed.ts

This creates all 23 tables and seeds the NMC,
CER, and INC reference data.

Verify it worked — open pgAdmin and check that
these tables exist and have data:
- nmc_database (should have 10+ rows)
- cer_database (should have 10+ rows)
- inc_database (should have 10+ rows)

──────────────────────────────────────────
STEP 3 — Setup registration backend
──────────────────────────────────────────
cd medlink-id-reg/backend

Create a .env file with this content:
NODE_ENV=development
PORT=5000
DATABASE_URL="postgresql://postgres:YOUR_PASSWORD@localhost:5432/medlink_db"
JWT_SECRET=medlink_jwt_secret_2024
JWT_REFRESH_SECRET=medlink_refresh_secret_2024
BCRYPT_ROUNDS=12

Then run:
npm install
npx prisma generate
npm run dev

Server should show:
MedLinkID Registration API running on http://localhost:5000

Test it:
Invoke-RestMethod -Uri "http://localhost:5000/api/v1/health"
Should return: status = healthy

──────────────────────────────────────────
STEP 4 — Setup registration frontend
──────────────────────────────────────────
cd medlink-id-reg/frontend

Create a .env.local file with this content:
NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL=http://localhost:5000/api/v1

Then run:
npm install
npm run dev

Frontend runs on http://localhost:3000

──────────────────────────────────────────
STEP 5 — Verify everything works
──────────────────────────────────────────
With both servers running, open the browser:

Test 1 — NMC validation
POST http://localhost:5000/api/v1/auth/validate-nmc
Body: { "nmcRegNumber": "TNMC20250001" }
Should return doctor details

Test 2 — Hospital registration
Open http://localhost:3000/register/hospital
Enter NMC: TNMC20250001
Enter CER: TN/CHN/2020/0001
Complete the solo registration flow
Should show Hospital ID and Doctor ID on success

──────────────────────────────────────────
WHAT IS WORKING
──────────────────────────────────────────
- Full hospital registration flow (solo clinic)
- Multi-staff registration flow (built, needs UI testing)
- NMC / CER / INC validation
- Patient registration API
- Account activation (/activate/[token])
- Login, refresh, logout

──────────────────────────────────────────
WHAT NEEDS TO BE DONE
──────────────────────────────────────────
- OTP integration (Fast2SMS)
- Patient registration form UI — photo field
  needs to be made optional
- UI polish across all pages
- Doctor portal (not started)
- Patient portal (not started)

──────────────────────────────────────────
IMPORTANT NOTES
──────────────────────────────────────────
- Never commit .env files
- The database on your machine is separate
  from Vishal's — that is correct and expected
- Both servers must run simultaneously:
  Backend on port 5000, Frontend on port 3000

That's everything. STEP 4 — OTP AND SESSION FLOW
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
Find every file related to the OTP consent flow.
The correct flow based on the schema is:

1. Doctor enters patientCode (format MLPR-XXXXXXXX)
2. System looks up Patient by patientCode
3. System creates AccessSession with status=PENDING_OTP
4. System creates OTPRecord with otpHash
5. OTP is sent to patient's phone via SMS
6. Doctor enters the OTP the patient reads out
7. System checks OTPRecord.otpHash, increments attempts
8. If correct: AccessSession.status → ACTIVE,
   AccessSession.startedAt = now()
9. Doctor can now view Patient and MedicalRecords
10. Session ends: status → ENDED_BY_DOCTOR or
    ENDED_BY_PATIENT or ENDED_BY_TIMEOUT
    AccessSession.endedAt = now(), endedBy = who ended it

For each step 1-10 tell me:
- Is it implemented? YES / PARTIAL / NO
- Which file and function handles it
- Any field name mismatches

import axios from 'axios';
// Dynamically pick API URL: if the browser is on localhost, use localhost.
// If on a LAN IP (e.g. mobile), use that same host so it reaches the backend.
function getBaseURL() {
  if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    const host = window.location.hostname;  // e.g. "localhost" or "192.168.1.4"
    return http://${host}:5000/api;
  }
  return process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:5000/api';
}
const api = axios.create({
  baseURL: getBaseURL(),
  headers: {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  },
});
// Add interceptor to inject Authorization header if token exists in localStorage
api.interceptors.request.use((config) => {
  if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
    const token = localStorage.getItem('doctorToken');
    if (token) {
      config.headers.Authorization = Bearer ${token};
    }
  }
  return config;
});
// Add response interceptor to handle expired/invalid tokens globally
api.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => response,
  (error) => {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      const status = error?.response?.status;
      if (status === 401 || status === 403) {
        // Check if this is a token auth error (not e.g. a patient access token error)
        const errorMsg = error?.response?.data?.error || '';
        const isTokenError =
          errorMsg.includes('expired') ||
          errorMsg.includes('Invalid') ||
          errorMsg.includes('Authentication required') ||
          status === 401;
        if (isTokenError) {
          localStorage.removeItem('doctorToken');
          localStorage.removeItem('doctorAuth');
          window.location.href = '/login';
        }
      }
    }
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);
export default api;Show moreMar 20Catalogued fifteen schema-backend mismatches and architectural gapsCatalogued fifteen schema-backend mismatches and architectural gapsI have everything I need. The controllers folder is empty — confirmed. All logic is inline in routes. Now here is the complete honest analysis of every bug before your teammate touches a single line.

Critical crashes — these will break immediately on first run:
1. licenseNo doesn't exist on Doctor model.
Used in authRoutes.ts and patientRoutes.ts everywhere — findUnique({ where: { licenseNo: doctorId } }), JWT payload { doctorId: doctor.licenseNo }. Schema has doctorCode and nmcRegNumber. Nothing called licenseNo.
2. specialty doesn't exist on Doctor model.
Used in accessRoutes.ts — doctor.specialty, session.doctor.specialty. Schema has specializationId (FK to Specialization table) with no direct string field.
3. PENDING_CONSENT status doesn't exist in AccessStatus enum.
Used throughout accessRoutes.ts. Schema enum values are: PENDING_OTP, ACTIVE, ENDED_BY_PATIENT, ENDED_BY_DOCTOR, ENDED_BY_TIMEOUT. PENDING_CONSENT is not one of them.
4. expiresAt doesn't exist on OTPRecord model.
accessRoutes.ts does prisma.oTPRecord.create({ data: { expiresAt: ... } }). Schema OTPRecord has no expiresAt field — only id, accessSessionId, otpHash, attempts, maxAttempts, verified, createdAt.
5. emergencyContact doesn't exist on Patient model.
patientRoutes.ts does select: { emergencyContact: true }. Schema has three separate fields: emergencyContactName, emergencyContactPhone, emergencyContactRelationship.
6. records relation doesn't exist on Patient.
patientRoutes.ts does include: { records: { ... } }. Schema relation is called medicalRecords.
7. doctor relation doesn't exist on MedicalRecord.
patientRoutes.ts does include: { hospital: true, doctor: true }. Schema relation is called uploadedByDoctor.
8. doctorId doesn't exist on FailedLoginAttempt.
authRoutes.ts does prisma.failedLoginAttempt.create({ data: { doctorId: doctor.id } }). Schema FailedLoginAttempt has userId not doctorId. Also failedLoginAttempt.count({ where: { doctorId: ... } }) — same wrong field.
9. AccessSession created without required fields.
Schema requires sessionToken (unique, not nullable), doctorSnapshot (Json, not nullable), and expiresAt (not nullable). accessRoutes.ts creates AccessSession without any of these three.
10. All audit log action strings are wrong.
auditLogger.ts logs actions like PATIENT_ACCESS_REQUESTED, PATIENT_CONSENT_GRANTED, LOGIN_SUCCESS, LOGIN_FAILED, EMERGENCY_ACCESS_GRANTED — none exist in the AuditAction enum. Valid values are: LOGIN, LOGOUT, VIEW_RECORD, CREATE_RECORD, UPDATE_RECORD, EMERGENCY_ACCESS, SESSION_STARTED, SESSION_ENDED, REGISTER_PATIENT.
11. dob used without null check in emergency endpoint.
calculateAge(patient.dob) — but dob is DateTime? (optional) in schema. Will crash if patient has no DOB.

Wrong provider — not a crash but needs fixing:
SMS uses Twilio. Project spec says Fast2SMS. Different API entirely.

What is missing entirely:

Medical records upload endpoint — no route exists
Medical records edit endpoint — no route exists
Session end endpoint — no route to close a session
logRoutes.ts — not yet read, need to check

  })

  })

  })

    data: { isDeleted: true, deletedAt: new Date() }
  })

Also update the GET /logs query to exclude soft-deleted:
  where: { doctorId: doctor.id, isDeleted: false }

Unearthed schema mismatch and charted database unification strategyThis is the root cause of everything. The doctor portal has its own separate schema — completely different from the unified one. # Fix 1 — specialization relation → use specializationId lookup instead

Missing endpoints — not built at all:

POST /patients/:id/records — upload a medical record (prescription, lab report, scan). No route, no controller, no file upload handling. The patient records page shows "No historical records" because there's no way to create them.
PUT /patients/:id/records/:recordId — edit a record's title or description. Schema has MedicalRecordEditAudit table ready but nothing writes to it.
DELETE /patients/:id/records/:recordId — soft delete a record. Schema has isDeleted field but no endpoint.
POST /access/end/:sessionId — doctor ends the session on patient departure. Schema has ENDED_BY_DOCTOR status and endedAt field but no endpoint to set them.
GET /patients/:id — get patient profile without records. Currently the only patient endpoint fetches records too. A separate lightweight endpoint for just the patient header info would be cleaner.

Missing backend logic in existing endpoints:

OTP attempt tracking — OTPRecord has attempts and maxAttempts fields but the verify endpoint never increments attempts or blocks after 3 wrong guesses.
Session expiry enforcement — AccessSession.expiresAt exists but nothing checks it server-side. An expired session token still works.

Not wired up:
8. EmergencyAccessLog table — emergency access creates an AccessSession but never writes to EmergencyAccessLog. Schema has a dedicated table for this.

════════════════════════════════════════════
FEATURE 1 — OTP ATTEMPT TRACKING
════════════════════════════════════════════
File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/accessRoutes.ts

In the POST /access/verify endpoint find where
wrong OTP is handled (isMatch === false).

Add this logic BEFORE the isMatch check:

1. Check if attempts >= maxAttempts:
   if (otpRecord.attempts >= otpRecord.maxAttempts) {
     await prisma.accessSession.update({
       where: { id: session.id },
       data: {
         status: 'ENDED_BY_TIMEOUT',
         endedAt: new Date(),
         endedBy: 'MAX_OTP_ATTEMPTS'
       }
     });
     return res.status(400).json({
       error: 'Too many incorrect attempts. Session cancelled. Please request a new OTP.'
     });
   }

2. When isMatch is false increment attempts:
   await prisma.oTPRecord.update({
     where: { id: otpRecord.id },
     data: { attempts: { increment: 1 } }
   });

Also do the same in POST /access/consent/:sessionId:
- Check attempts >= maxAttempts before verifying
- Increment attempts when OTP is wrong

After writing show me the updated verify endpoint.
Say FEATURE 1 DONE when complete.

════════════════════════════════════════════
FEATURE 2 — SESSION END ENDPOINT
════════════════════════════════════════════
File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/accessRoutes.ts

Add this new route after the existing /verify endpoint:

POST /access/end/:sessionId
Requires: authenticateDoctor middleware
Purpose: Doctor closes session when patient leaves

Logic:
1. Get sessionId from req.params.sessionId
2. Get doctorToken from (req as any).doctor
3. Find the doctor: prisma.doctor.findFirst
   where: { doctorCode: doctorToken.doctorId }
4. Find the session: prisma.accessSession.findUnique
   where: { id: sessionId }
   Check: session must exist AND status must be ACTIVE
   AND session.doctorId must equal doctor.id
   If not found or not ACTIVE return 404
   If doctorId does not match return 403
5. Update the session:
   prisma.accessSession.update
   where: { id: sessionId }
   data: {
     status: 'ENDED_BY_DOCTOR',
     endedAt: new Date(),
     endedBy: 'DOCTOR'
   }
6. Log the action:
   logDoctorAction(doctor.id, 'SESSION_ENDED',
   session.patientId, 'PATIENT', req, {
     sessionId: session.id,
     endedBy: 'DOCTOR'
   })
7. Return: { message: 'Session ended successfully' }

After writing show me the new route code.
Say FEATURE 2 DONE when complete.

════════════════════════════════════════════
FEATURE 3 — SESSION EXPIRY ENFORCEMENT
════════════════════════════════════════════
File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/patientRoutes.ts

In the GET /:id/records endpoint, after finding
the patient with findUnique, add this check
BEFORE returning any data:

Find the active session for this doctor+patient:
const doctorToken = (req as any).doctor;
const doctor = await prisma.doctor.findFirst({
  where: { doctorCode: doctorToken.doctorId }
});

const activeSession = await prisma.accessSession.findFirst({
  where: {
    patientId: patientData.id,
    doctorId: doctor.id,
    status: 'ACTIVE'
  },
  orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' }
});

if (!activeSession) {
  return res.status(403).json({
    error: 'No active session. Request OTP first.'
  });
}

if (new Date() > activeSession.expiresAt) {
  await prisma.accessSession.update({
    where: { id: activeSession.id },
    data: {
      status: 'ENDED_BY_TIMEOUT',
      endedAt: new Date(),
      endedBy: 'TIMEOUT'
    }
  });
  return res.status(403).json({
    error: 'Session has expired. Please request a new OTP.'
  });
}

After writing show me the updated records endpoint.

FEATURE 5 — MEDICAL RECORDS UPLOAD
════════════════════════════════════════════
File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/patientRoutes.ts

Add this new route:

POST /patients/:id/records
Requires: authenticateDoctor middleware
Purpose: Upload a medical record for a patient

First install multer for file handling:
npm install multer @types/multer

Then add at top of patientRoutes.ts:
import multer from 'multer';
import path from 'path';
import fs from 'fs';

const uploadDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads', 'records');
if (!fs.existsSync(uploadDir)) {
  fs.mkdirSync(uploadDir, { recursive: true });
}

const storage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: (req, file, cb) => cb(null, uploadDir),
  filename: (req, file, cb) => {
    const uniqueName = `${Date.now()}-${Math.random().toString(36).slice(2)}${path.extname(file.originalname)}`;
    cb(null, uniqueName);
  }
});

const upload = multer({
  storage,
  limits: { fileSize: 5 * 1024 * 1024 },
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    const allowed = ['image/jpeg', 'image/png', 'application/pdf'];
    if (allowed.includes(file.mimetype)) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(new Error('Only JPEG, PNG, and PDF files are allowed'));
    }
  }
});

Route logic:
router.post('/:id/records',
  authenticateDoctor,
  upload.single('file'),
  async (req, res) => {
    const patientCode = req.params.id;
    const { recordType, title, description } = req.body;
    const doctorToken = (req as any).doctor;

    if (!req.file) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'File is required' });
    }

    const patient = await prisma.patient.findUnique({
      where: { patientCode }
    });
    if (!patient) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Patient not found' });
    }

    const doctor = await prisma.doctor.findFirst({
      where: { doctorCode: doctorToken.doctorId }
    });
    if (!doctor) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Doctor not found' });
    }

    const validTypes = [
      'PRESCRIPTION', 'LAB_REPORT', 'SCAN',
      'DIAGNOSIS', 'DISCHARGE_SUMMARY'
    ];
    if (!validTypes.includes(recordType)) {
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Invalid record type. Must be one of: ' + validTypes.join(', ')
      });
    }

    const record = await prisma.medicalRecord.create({
      data: {
        patientId: patient.id,
        hospitalId: doctor.hospitalId,
        uploadedByRole: 'DOCTOR',
        uploadedByDoctorId: doctor.id,
        uploadedByName: doctor.name,
        recordType: recordType,
        title: title,
        description: description || null,
        fileUrl: `/uploads/records/${req.file.filename}`,
        fileKey: req.file.filename,
        fileMimeType: req.file.mimetype,
        fileSizeBytes: req.file.size,
      }
    });

    await logDoctorAction(doctor.id, 'CREATE_RECORD',
      record.id, 'MedicalRecord', req, {
        patientCode: patient.patientCode,
        recordType,
        title
      }
    );

    return res.status(201).json({
      message: 'Record uploaded successfully',
      record
    });
  }
);

Also add this to server.ts to serve uploaded files:
import express from 'express'; (already imported)
app.use('/uploads', express.static(
  path.join(process.cwd(), 'uploads')
));

FEATURE 6 — MEDICAL RECORDS EDIT
════════════════════════════════════════════
File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/patientRoutes.ts

Add this new route:

PUT /patients/:id/records/:recordId
Requires: authenticateDoctor middleware
Purpose: Edit title and description of a record

Logic:
1. Find patient by patientCode (req.params.id)
2. Find record by id (req.params.recordId)
   where: { id: recordId, patientId: patient.id,
             isDeleted: false }
3. Find doctor by doctorCode
4. Get { title, description, reason } from req.body
5. Store old values before update
6. Update record:
   prisma.medicalRecord.update
   where: { id: recordId }
   data: {
     title: title || record.title,
     description: description ?? record.description,
     lastEditedAt: new Date(),
     lastEditedById: doctor.id,
     lastEditedByRole: 'DOCTOR',
     lastEditedByName: doctor.name,
   }
7. Write to MedicalRecordEditAudit for each
   changed field:
   If title changed:
     prisma.medicalRecordEditAudit.create({
       data: {
         medicalRecordId: recordId,
         editedByRole: 'DOCTOR',
         editedByDoctorId: doctor.id,
         editedByName: doctor.name,
         fieldChanged: 'title',
         oldValue: record.title,
         newValue: title,
         hospitalId: doctor.hospitalId,
         reason: reason || null,
       }
     })
   If description changed: same pattern
8. Log: logDoctorAction(doctor.id, 'UPDATE_RECORD',
   recordId, 'MedicalRecord', req, { reason })
9. Return updated record

After writing show me the new route.

Now build FEATURE 2 — SESSION END ENDPOINT.

File to edit:
medlink-id-docter/backend/src/routes/accessRoutes.ts

Add this new route after the existing /verify endpoint:

router.post('/end/:sessionId', authenticateDoctor, async (req: Request, res: Response): Promise<any> => {
  try {
    const sessionId = req.params.sessionId as string;
    const doctorToken = (req as any).doctor;

    const doctor = await prisma.doctor.findFirst({
      where: { doctorCode: doctorToken.doctorId }
    });
    if (!doctor) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Doctor not found' });
    }

    const session = await prisma.accessSession.findUnique({
      where: { id: sessionId }
    });

    if (!session) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'Session not found' });
    }

    if (session.status !== 'ACTIVE') {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Session is not active' });
    }

    if (session.doctorId !== doctor.id) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'You do not have permission to end this session' });
    }

    await prisma.accessSession.update({
      where: { id: sessionId },
      data: {
        status: 'ENDED_BY_DOCTOR',
        endedAt: new Date(),
        endedBy: 'DOCTOR'
      }
    });

    await logDoctorAction(doctor.id, 'SESSION_ENDED', session.patientId, 'PATIENT', req, {
      sessionId: session.id,
      endedBy: 'DOCTOR'
    });

    return res.json({ message: 'Session ended successfully' });

  } catch (error) {
    console.error('End session error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error' });
  }
});
